Func LAUDAIMA()
	If Not $g_bComboSent Then
		_SendComboOnce()
	EndIf
	GUICtrlSetData($CRACK, "10")
_LAUDAIMA()  ;Checkpoint 158
	Local $start = TimerInit()
	While TimerDiff($start) < 1
		_MEMORYPOINTERWRITE($FINALADDRESS, $HMEMORY, $OFFSET1, "1066597109")
		_MEMORYPOINTERWRITE($FINALADDRESS, $HMEMORY, $OFFSET2, "1078765678")
		_MEMORYPOINTERWRITE($FINALADDRESS, $HMEMORY, $OFFSET3, "1076524948")
	WEnd
